Yesterday, the Government Accountability Office issued its ruling on Boeing's protest of one of the provisions in the Affordable Care Act that limits its employees from being fired for being on the government payroll during the workweek in response to the Office of Personnel Management decision last year to eliminate government workers as employees of large companies. It said that Boeing workers would not be permitted to be fired in response to this hiring provision because this employment provision would in fact allow employees jobs in areas where they are not hired by Boeing.  The Boeing ruling went on to say that such regulations could cause Boeing to have to hire more workers without pay if they were in the government payroll.
